<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:muil.html>muil</a> (15515)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">muul</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">mūl</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mūlą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muil.html>muil</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muilen.html>muilen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muiltje.html>muiltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An animal's mouth and muzzle or snout
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:temmer.html>temmer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:steekt.html>steekt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:muil.html>muil</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leeuw.html>leeuw</a></i>
<dl><dd><i>The tamer puts his head in the lion's mouth</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person's face</li>
<li>(<i>notably in <a href = vnd.unilang:muilen.html>muilen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:trekken.html>trekken</a></i>) A funny, angry ... face one <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a>, facial expression</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snuit.html>snuit</a></span></li>
<li>(<i>person's face</i>) <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelaat.html>gelaat</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gezicht.html>gezicht</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smoel.html>smoel</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">muul</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">(calceus) mulleus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">red shoe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muil.html>muil</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muilen.html>muilen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muiltje.html>muiltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>(<i>usually as plural diminutive <b>muiltjes</b></i>) A <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> type of footwear
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> sprookjesprins <a href = vnd.unilang:zocht.html>zocht</a> Assepoester <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanwijzing.html>aanwijzing</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:glazen.html>glazen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:muiltje.html>muiltje</a></b></i>
<dl><dd><i>The fairytale prince looked for Cideralla with her glass slipper as only clue</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">muul</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mūlus</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muil.html>muil</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muilen.html>muilen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muiltje.html>muiltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:muildier.html>muildier</a> (28619)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muil.html>muil</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mule</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muildier.html>muildier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muildieren.html>muildieren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muildier.html>muildiertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>mule (the sterile hybrid offspring of a male donkey or ass (he-ass, <a href = vnd.unilang:jackass.html>jackass</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a>) and a female horse (mare))</li></ol>

<p>From the <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muiten.html>muiten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mutiny</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-erij</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Or alternatively, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muiter.html>muiter</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mutineer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ij</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">muyseval</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*mūsfalla</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*mūsfallā</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muis.html>muis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mouse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:val.html>val</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:trap.html>trap</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">mulato</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">mulato</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mūlus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mule</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Etymologically related to Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muil.html>muil</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mule</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muildier.html>muildier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mule</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***mulberry-tree.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> mulberry-tree</h1><br><a href = vnd.unilang:moerbei.html>moerbei</a><br><a href = vnd.unilang:moerbeiboom.html>moerbeiboom</a><br></body> 
***mulberry.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mulberry.html>mulberry</a> (74186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">Mulbery</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">molberye</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">murberie</i>, partly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mōrberiġe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:mulberry.html>mulberry</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and partly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">mulbere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:mulberry.html>mulberry</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">moerbezie</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moerbei.html>moerbei</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:mulberry.html>mulberry</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Maulbeere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:mulberry.html>mulberry</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mulberry.html>mulberry</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mulberries</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of several trees, of the genus <i>Morus</i>, having edible fruits.
<ul><li><b>1837</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:luigi.html>Luigi</a> Tinelli, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hints.html>Hints</a> on the Cultivation of the <a href = vnd.unilang:mulberry.html>Mulberry</a>, with Some General Observations on the Production of Silk</i>, page 39:
<dl><dd>Different qualities of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mulberry.html>Mulberry</a></b>. Among the different species of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mulberry.html>Mulberry</a></b>, it  <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ascei'tained that the Italian, (Morus italica) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> eaten by the silk worm, with eager  appetite. It's fruit <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> very small, and of a pale <a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a> colour.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>The fruit of this tree.
<ul><li><b>2010</b>, Geoff Stebbings, <i>Growing Your Own Fruit and Veg For <a href = vnd.unilang:dummies.html>Dummies</a></i>, John Wiley amp; Sons (→ISBN)
<dl><dd>You can also make good jam with <b>mulberries</b>, and they taste great cooked or  mixed together with other fruits. <b>Mulberries</b> are rich in sugar with moderate  amounts of vitamin C. Their rich colours are a sign that they contain high levels of <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A dark purple colour tinted with red.
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel"><a href = vnd.unilang:mulberry.html>mulberry</a> colour: <span style="background-color:78184A; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***mullet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mullet.html>mullet</a> (59979)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Mullet_at_Port_Erin_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1703217.jpg/220px-Mullet_at_Port_Erin_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1703217.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Mullet_at_Port_Erin_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1703217.jpg/330px-Mullet_at_Port_Erin_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1703217.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Mullet_at_Port_Erin_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1703217.jpg/440px-Mullet_at_Port_Erin_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1703217.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3296" data-file-height="2472" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:mullet.html>Mullet</a> catch</div></div></div>
<div class="sister-wikispecies sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: solid aaa 1px; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;">
<div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Wikispecies-logo.svg/50px-Wikispecies-logo.svg.png" decoding="async" width="50" height="59" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Wikispecies-logo.svg/75px-Wikispecies-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Wikispecies-logo.svg/100px-Wikispecies-logo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="941" data-file-height="1103" /></div></div>
<div style="margin-left: 60px;"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikispecies" class="extiw" title="w:Wikispecies">Wikispecies</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> information on:
<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><i><b><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Mugilidae" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Mugilidae">Mugilidae</a></b></i></div>
</div></div>
<p><span class="interProject"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Mugilidae" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Mugilidae">Wikispecies <sup></sup></a></span>
From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">mulet</i> (now ‘grey <a href = vnd.unilang:mullet.html>mullet</a>’), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mullus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">red <a href = vnd.unilang:mullet.html>mullet</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μύλλος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">múllos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mullet.html>mullet</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mullets</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:mullet.html>mullet</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A fish of the family Mullidae (order Syngnathiformes), especially the genus <i>Mullus</i> (the red mullets or goatfish).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">especially <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fish of the family Mugilidae (order Mugiliformes) (the grey mullets).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of several species of freshwater fish in the sucker family (especially in the genus <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Moxostoma" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Moxostoma"><i>Moxostoma</i></a></span>, the redhorses)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Mugillidae</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">haarder</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Mugillidae</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">springer</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Or mullethead, possibly derived from the fish (see Etymology 1) or from <i>mull</i> (meaning <i>to stupefy</i>) though neither <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> certain.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mullet.html>mullet</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mullets</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A fool</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mullet_(haircut)" class="extiw" title="w:Mullet (haircut)"><a href = vnd.unilang:mullet.html>Mullet</a> (haircut)</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mullet_(haircut)" class="extiw" title="w:Mullet (haircut)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<div class="thumb tmulti tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:204px;max-width:204px"><div class="tsingle" style="margin:1px;width:202px;max-width:202px"><div class="thumbimage"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/David_Bowie_-_TopPop_1974_03.png/200px-David_Bowie_-_TopPop_1974_03.png" decoding="async" width="200" height="198" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/David_Bowie_-_TopPop_1974_03.png/300px-David_Bowie_-_TopPop_1974_03.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/David_Bowie_-_TopPop_1974_03.png/400px-David_Bowie_-_TopPop_1974_03.png 2x" data-file-width="500" data-file-height="494" /></div><div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left">David <a href = vnd.unilang:bowie.html>Bowie</a> with a <a href = vnd.unilang:mullet.html>mullet</a> hairstyle.</div></div><div class="tsingle" style="margin:1px;width:202px;max-width:202px"><div class="thumbimage"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/SuperMullet.jpg/200px-SuperMullet.jpg" decoding="async" width="200" height="287" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/SuperMullet.jpg/300px-SuperMullet.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/SuperMullet.jpg/400px-SuperMullet.jpg 2x" data-file-width="522" data-file-height="750" /></div><div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a> with a long <a href = vnd.unilang:mullet.html>mullet</a> hairstyle.</div></div></div></div>
<p>1994 US. Coined and popularized by hip hop group the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beastie_Boys" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Beastie Boys">Beastie Boys</a> in their song "<a href = vnd.unilang:mullet.html>Mullet</a> Head".
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mullet.html>mullet</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mullets</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A hairstyle where the hair <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> kept short on the top and sides and long at the back.
<ul><li><b>1994</b>, Beastie Boys "<a href = vnd.unilang:mullet.html>Mullet</a> Head"
<dl><dd>– <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mullet.html>Mullet</a></b> head, don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> touch the back</dd>
<dd>– Cut the sides, don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> touch the back</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2008</b>, Danielle Corsetto, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.daniellecorsetto.com/GWS406.html"><a href = vnd.unilang:girls.html>Girls</a> With Slingshots 406</a>
<dl><dd>– Maybe it's a <a href = vnd.unilang:curly.html>curly</a> fro.</dd>
<dd>– Maybe every day <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> bad hair day!</dd>
<dd>– Maybe it's a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mullet.html>mullet</a></b>!</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person who mindlessly follows a fad, a trend, or a leader.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">hockey hair</span></li></ul>

***munitie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:munitie.html>munitie</a> (3358)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">munire</i> 'to equip'.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:munitie.html>munitie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">ammunition</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">munition</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">sharp</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">remark</span>s with which to <span class="Latn" lang="en">assault</span> someone</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Often wrongly pronounced as <i>menutie</i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:munt.html>munt</a> (4473)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:munten.html>munte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">munita</i>, from late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*munit</i>,, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">monēta</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:munt.html>munt</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:munten.html>munten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muntje.html>muntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>coin

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mente</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">minte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mentha</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>mint <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">plant</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, of genus <i>Mentha</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> confection flavored with mint</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:munten.html>munten</a> (6567)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:munten.html>munten</a></i>, from Germanic. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">münten</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">muntsje</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">mintsje</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">münzen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mint</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to intend, purpose</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">mint</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:murw.html>murwe</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">morwe</i>, variant forms of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">meru</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">merue</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soft, tender, weak</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*marwaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">mürbe</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">meru</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mearu</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soft, tender</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">mellow</span>.

***mus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mus.html>mus</a> (20738)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mussche</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">musca</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">muscio</i>, derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">musca</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Limburgish" class="extiw" title="w:Limburgish">Limburgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="li">mösj</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Central_Franconian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Central Franconian language">Central Franconian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-cfr">Mösch, Mesch</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luxembourgish" class="extiw" title="w:Luxembourgish">Luxembourgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">Mësch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mus.html>mus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mussen.html>mussen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:musje.html>musje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sparrow, bird of the family Passeridae, especially of the genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:passer.html>Passer</a></i> and a few <a href = vnd.unilang:smaller.html>smaller</a> genera</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:mus.html>mus</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:vogels.html>vogels</a>)</span> <a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Passeridae" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Passeridae"><span style="color:green;"><i>Passeridae</i></span></a> <img alt="op Wikispecies" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/14px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/21px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/28px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 2x" data-file-width="125" data-file-height="160" />, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zangvogel.html>zangvogel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:behorend.html>behorend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> wevervogels <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zelden.html>zelden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ver.html>ver</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nestelt.html>nestelt</a>.

***mush.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a> (45024)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably a variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mash</i>, or from a dialectal variant of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:mos.html>mos</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a>, pulp, porridge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">appelmos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">applesauce</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mōs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">food, victuals, porridge, <a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*mōs</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mōsą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">porridge, food</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*meh₂d-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a>, fat, dripping</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">moosh</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moes.html>moes</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pulp, <a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a>, porridge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:mus.html>Mus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jam, <a href = vnd.unilang:puree.html>puree</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:mos.html>mos</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pulp, mash, <a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also moose.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mushes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A somewhat liquid mess, often of food; a soft or semisolid substance.
<ul><li><b>1855</b>, Frederick Douglass, <i>My Bondage and My Freedom</i> Chapter 1
<dl><dd>His food <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> of the coarsest <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a>, consisting for the most part of cornmeal <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></b>, which often finds its way from the wooden tray to his mouth in an oyster shell.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">radio</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A mixture of noise produced by the harmonics of continuous-wave <a href = vnd.unilang:stations.html>stations</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">surfing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The foam of a breaker.
<ul><li><b>2008</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bucky.html>Bucky</a> McMahon, <i>Night Diver</i> (page 80)
<dl><dd>And Rincon <i><a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a></i> all about surfing. Flash back thirty-odd years, to a skinny kid on a <a href = vnd.unilang:styrofoam.html>Styrofoam</a> belly-board, pin-wheeling out into the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></b> of Jacksonville Beach, Florida.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A magmatic body containing a significant proportion of <a href = vnd.unilang:crystals.html>crystals</a> suspended in the liquid phase or melt.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">mushes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mushing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mushed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To squish so as to break into <a href = vnd.unilang:smaller.html>smaller</a> pieces or to combine with something else.
<dl><dd><i>He <b>mushed</b> the ingredients together.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">muos</i> and <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Goidelic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Goidelic languages">Goidelic</a></span></span> <i class="Zyyy mention" lang="und"><a href = vnd.unilang:mus.html>mus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a <a href = vnd.unilang:pap.html>pap</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Zyyy mention" lang="und"><a href = vnd.unilang:muss.html>muss</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a porridge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or any thick preparation of fruit.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>A food comprising cracked or rolled grains cooked in water or milk; porridge.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rural  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Cornmeal cooked in water and served as a porridge or as a thick sidedish like grits or mashed potatoes.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Believed to be a contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a> on</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michif" class="extiw" title="w:Michif">Michif</a></span>, in turn a corruption of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">marchons!</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">marche!</i>, the cry of the voyageurs and <a href = vnd.unilang:coureurs.html>coureurs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bois.html>bois</a> to their dogs.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">A directive given (usually to dogs or a horse) to start moving, or to move faster.</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mushes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A walk, especially across the snow with dogs.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">mushes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mushing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mushed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To walk, especially across the snow with dogs.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To drive dogs, usually pulling a sled, across the snow.
<ul><li><b>1910</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>Jack</a> London, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Burning_Daylight" class="extiw" title="s:Burning Daylight">Burning Daylight</a></i>, <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Burning_Daylight/Part_I_Chapter_IV" class="extiw" title="s:Burning Daylight/Part I Chapter IV">part 1 chapter 4</a>:
<dl><dd>Together the two <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> loaded and lashed the sled. They warmed their hands for the last time, pulled on their <a href = vnd.unilang:mittens.html>mittens</a>, and <b>mushed</b> the dogs <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the bank and down to the river-trail.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Simple contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mushroom</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mushes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Quebec<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A magic mushroom.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">shroom</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology 5</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Angloromani_language" class="extiw" title="w:Angloromani language">Angloromani</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="rme"><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Romani_language" class="extiw" title="w:Romani language">Romani</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="rom">mursh</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">मनुष्य</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">manuṣya</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">human being, <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mushes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_England" class="extiw" title="w:Southern England">Southern England</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">A form of address to a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mate.html>mate</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">UK</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">pal</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">especially US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote?)</span>  “MAUREEN AND DOREEN AND NOREEN AND ME”, in  <cite>Peculiar Poems</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.jclamb.com">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">'Oy, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></b>! Get out of it!' / That's what <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a>'d say / Barging the locals / Out of the way</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote?)</span>  “THE ONCE AND FUTURE KING: In Which King Arthur <a href = vnd.unilang:uther.html>Uther</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pendragon.html>Pendragon</a> Grants An Interview”, in <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20050405195144/http://arthurpendragon.ukonline.co.uk/arthur.html">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">When I'm around it's not uncommon for someone to call <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> and say :'Oy <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></b>, get your bum <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> here and give us a hand.'</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_England" class="extiw" title="w:Northern England">Northern England</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The face.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">mug</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology 6</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">moucheter</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut with small <a href = vnd.unilang:cuts.html>cuts</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mush.html>mush</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">mushes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mushing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mushed</b>)

***musicus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:musicus.html>musicus</a> (18015)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mūsicus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:musicus.html>musicus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:musici.html>musici</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:musicus.html>musicusje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>musician (a person who plays or <a href = vnd.unilang:sings.html>sings</a> music)</li></ol>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:musicus.html>musicus</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:muziek.html>muziek</a>)</span>, <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:beroep.html>beroep</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muziek.html>muziek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maakt.html>maakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> ten <a href = vnd.unilang:gehore.html>gehore</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brengt.html>brengt</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:musici.html>musici</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zwaaien.html>zwaaien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verlaten.html>verlaten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>Groot</a>: „Deze <a href = vnd.unilang:meneer.html>meneer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:probeerde.html>probeerde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ene.html>ene</a> hand <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:krijgen.html>krijgen</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:misschien.html>Misschien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klappen.html>klappen</a>.” <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verpleegkundige.html>verpleegkundige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begint.html>begint</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gesprekje.html>gesprekje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> patiënt <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> gespeelde <a href = vnd.unilang:muziek.html>muziek</a>.  <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup></i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***musk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:musk.html>musk</a> (63881)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">muske</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">musc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">muscus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μόσχος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">móskhos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Persian" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Persian">Middle Persian</a></span> <small>[script needed]</small> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="pal-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mwšk'</span> <span class="ts mention-ts Latn">/mušk/</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">مشک</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mošk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">मुष्क</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">muṣka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">testicle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the shape of the gland of animals secreting the substance being compared to human testicles, a diminutive of <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">मूष्</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mūṣ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mouse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the shape of human testicles being compared to mice, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*muh₂s</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mouse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with mouse.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:musk.html>musk</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">musks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A greasy secretion with a powerful odour, produced in a glandular sac of the male <a href = vnd.unilang:musk.html>musk</a> deer and used in the manufacture of perfumes.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1607</b>,  [attributed to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Tomkis" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Thomas Tomkis">Thomas Tomkis</a>],  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lingua_(play)" class="extiw" title="w:Lingua (play)">Lingva: Or The Combat of the Tongue, and the Five Senses for Superiority. A Pleasant Comœdie.</a></cite>, London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_Eld" class="extiw" title="w:George Eld">G[eorge] <a href = vnd.unilang:eld.html>Eld</a></a>, for <a href = vnd.unilang:simon.html>Simon</a> Waterson, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/52434902">52434902</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=u1dOAQAAMAAJamp;pg=PP138">Act IV, scene iii</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Your onely way to make a good pomander, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> this. Take an ownce of the pureſt garden mould, clenſed and ſteeped ſeauen daies in change of motherleſſe roſe water, then take the beſt Labdanum, Benioine, both Storaxes, <a href = vnd.unilang:amber.html>amber</a> greece, and Ciuet, and <b>muſke</b>, incorporate them together, and work them into what form you pleaſe; this, if your breath bee not to valiant, will make you ſmell as ſweete as my <a href = vnd.unilang:ladies.html>Ladies</a> dogge.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A similar secretion produced by the otter and the civet.</li>
<li>A synthetic organic compound used as a substitute for the above.</li>
<li>The odour of <a href = vnd.unilang:musk.html>musk</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href = vnd.unilang:musk.html>musk</a> deer (genus <i>Moschus</i>).</li>
<li>The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/musk_plant" class="extiw" title="w:musk plant"><a href = vnd.unilang:musk.html>musk</a> plant</a> (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Mimulus_moschatus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Mimulus moschatus"><i>Mimulus moschatus</i></a></span>).</li>
<li>A plant of the genus <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Erodium" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Erodium"><i>Erodium</i></a></span> (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Erodium_moschatum" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Erodium moschatum"><i>Erodium moschatum</i></a></span>); the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/musky_heronsbill" class="extiw" title="w:musky heronsbill">musky heronsbill</a>.</li>
<li>A plant of the genus <i>Muscari</i>; grape hyacinth.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The scent of human genitalia when aroused or unwashed.
<dl><dd><i>I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> so excited I could smell my own <b><a href = vnd.unilang:musk.html>musk</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:muscat.html>muscat</a></span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:musk.html>musk</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">musks</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">musking</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">musked</b>)

***muskiet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:muskiet.html>muskiet</a> (59974)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">mosquito</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gnat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, diminutive of Spanish <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:mosca.html>mosca</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">musca</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mūs-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fly, stinging fly, gnat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with West-Flemish <i class="Latn mention" lang="vls">meuzie</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mosquito</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span></span> dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">mausa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mosquito</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">musė</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a fly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:midge.html>midge</a></span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muskiet.html>muskiet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muskieten.html>muskieten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muskiet.html>muskietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>tropical <span class="Latn" lang="en">mosquito</span>es that feed on <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nectar.html>nectar</a></span>s (compare <span class="Latn" lang="nl">mug</span>)</li>
<li>any species of <span class="Latn" lang="en">mosquito</span> (not scientifically correct, but generally accepted)</li></ol>

</p>
